-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Schema LeeAnneVineyard
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard` DEFAULT CHARACTER SET utf8 ;
USE `LeeAnneVineyard` ;

-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`bottle`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`bottle` (
  `idBottle` INT(5) NOT NULL,
  `BottleCapacity` INT(3) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `BottleShape` VARCHAR(20) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `BottleColor` VARCHAR(45) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `BottlePrice` DECIMAL(4,2) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `BottleInvCount` INT(4) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idBottle`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`employee`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`employee` (
  `idEmployee` INT(11) NOT NULL,
  `EmployeePosition` VARCHAR(30) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `EmployeeSupID` INT(11) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `EmployeeFn` VARCHAR(15) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `EmployeeLn` VARCHAR(15) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `EmployeSocSec` INT(11) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `EmployeeAddress` VARCHAR(45) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `EmployeePhone` VARCHAR(12) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idEmployee`),
  INDEX `fk_Employee_Employee1_idx` (`EmployeeSupID` ASC),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_Employee_Employee1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`EmployeeSupID`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`employee` (`idEmployee`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`wine`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`wine` (
  `idWine` INT(11) NOT NULL,
  `WineName` VARCHAR(20) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `Employee_idEmployee` INT(11) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `BarrelType` VARCHAR(25) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `PercAlcohol` DECIMAL(2,2) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `AgingRequirement` INT(2) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `WineCategory` VARCHAR(25) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idWine`),
  INDEX `fk_Wine_Employee1_idx` (`Employee_idEmployee` ASC),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_Wine_Employee1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`Employee_idEmployee`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`employee` (`idEmployee`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`product`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`product` (
  `idProduct` INT(4) NOT NULL,
  `idBottle` INT(5) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `idWine` INT(3) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `CasePrice` DECIMAL(6,2) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `BottleQuantity` INT(2) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idProduct`),
  INDEX `fk_idBottle1` (`idBottle` ASC),
  INDEX `fk_idWine` (`idWine` ASC),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_idBottle1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`idBottle`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`bottle` (`idBottle`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_idWine`
    FOREIGN KEY (`idWine`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`wine` (`idWine`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`customer`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`customer` (
  `idCustomer` INT(3) NOT NULL,
  `CustomerType` VARCHAR(15) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `CustomerAddress` VARCHAR(45) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `CustomerPhone` VARCHAR(12) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idCustomer`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`cus_order`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`cus_order` (
  `idCus_Order` INT(11) NOT NULL,
  `Customer_idCustomer` INT(11) NOT NULL,
  `OrderRecDate` DATE NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `ShipDate` DATE NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idCus_Order`, `Customer_idCustomer`),
  INDEX `fk_Cus_Order_Customer1_idx` (`Customer_idCustomer` ASC),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_Cus_Order_Customer1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`Customer_idCustomer`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`customer` (`idCustomer`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`case_has_cus_order`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`case_has_cus_order` (
  `idProduct` INT(11) NOT NULL,
  `idCus_Order` INT(11) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idProduct`, `idCus_Order`),
  INDEX `fk_Case_has_Cus_Order_Cus_Order1_idx` (`idCus_Order` ASC),
  INDEX `fk_Case_has_Cus_Order_Case1_idx` (`idProduct` ASC),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_Case_has_Cus_Order_Case1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`idProduct`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`product` (`idProduct`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_Case_has_Cus_Order_Cus_Order1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`idCus_Order`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`cus_order` (`idCus_Order`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;

ENGINE = InnoDB

-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`glass_vendor`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`glass_vendor` (
  `idGlass_Vendor` INT(11) NOT NULL,
  `VendorName` VARCHAR(25) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `VendorPOC` VARCHAR(20) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `VendorAddress` VARCHAR(45) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `VendorCity` VARCHAR(25) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `VendorState` VARCHAR(2) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `VendorPostalCode` INT(5) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `VendorPhone` BIGINT(10) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idGlass_Vendor`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`grape`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`grape` (
  `idGrape` VARCHAR(3) NOT NULL,
  `GrapeName` VARCHAR(25) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idGrape`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`juice`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`juice` (
  `Grape_idGrape` VARCHAR(3) NOT NULL,
  `Wine_idWine` INT(11) NOT NULL,
  `Conversion_Ratio` INT(3) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `GrapeProportion` DECIMAL(3,2) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`Wine_idWine`, `Grape_idGrape`),
  INDEX `fk_Juice_Grape_idx` (`Grape_idGrape` ASC),
  INDEX `fk_Juice_Wine1_idx` (`Wine_idWine` ASC),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_Juice_Grape`
    FOREIGN KEY (`Grape_idGrape`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`grape` (`idGrape`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_Juice_Wine1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`Wine_idWine`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`wine` (`idWine`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`vendor_orders`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`vendor_orders` (
  `idOrder` INT(4) NOT NULL,
  `idGlass_Vendor` INT(2) NOT NULL,
  `idBottle` INT(5) NOT NULL,
  `BottleOrderedQuantity` INT(3) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `BottleReceivedQuantity` INT(3) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `OrderDate` DATE NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `ReceivedDate` DATE NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idOrder`, `idGlass_Vendor`, `idBottle`),
  INDEX `fk_Vendor_Orders_Glass_Vendor1_idx` (`idGlass_Vendor` ASC),
  INDEX `fk_idBottle_idx` (`idBottle` ASC),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_Vendor_Orders_Glass_Vendor1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`idGlass_Vendor`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`glass_vendor` (`idGlass_Vendor`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_idBottle`
    FOREIGN KEY (`idBottle`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`bottle` (`idBottle`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`vineyard`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`vineyard` (
  `idVineyard` INT(2) NOT NULL,
  `VineyardName` VARCHAR(15) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `VineyardSize` INT(11) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `VineyardAddress` VARCHAR(40) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `VineyardCity` VARCHAR(25) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `Employee_idEmployee` INT(11) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idVineyard`),
  INDEX `fk_Vineyard_Employee1_idx` (`Employee_idEmployee` ASC),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_employeeid`
    FOREIGN KEY (`Employee_idEmployee`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`employee` (`idEmployee`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`vintage`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`vintage` (
  `VintageYear` INT(4) NOT NULL,
  `Grape_idGrape` VARCHAR(3) NOT NULL,
  `HarvestAmount` DECIMAL(10,0) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `HarvestRipeness` DECIMAL(2,2) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`VintageYear`, `Grape_idGrape`),
  INDEX `fk_Grape_idGrape_idx` (`Grape_idGrape` ASC),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_Grape_idGrape`
    FOREIGN KEY (`Grape_idGrape`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`grape` (`idGrape`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `LeeAnneVineyard`.`vineyard_planting`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `LeeAnneVineyard`.`vineyard_planting` (
  `idVineyard` INT(11) NOT NULL,
  `VintageYear` INT(4) NOT NULL,
  `Grape_idGrape` VARCHAR(3) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idVineyard`, `VintageYear`, `Grape_idGrape`),
  INDEX `fk_Grape_idGrape1_idx` (`Grape_idGrape` ASC),
  INDEX `fk_VintageYear1_idx` (`VintageYear` ASC),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_Grape_idGrape1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`Grape_idGrape`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`vintage` (`Grape_idGrape`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_VintageYear1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`VintageYear`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`vintage` (`VintageYear`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_idVineyard`
    FOREIGN KEY (`idVineyard`)
    REFERENCES `LeeAnneVineyard`.`vineyard` (`idVineyard`))
ENGINE = InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET = utf8;
